Selected games of the Togyzqumalaq 
Championship of the Republic of 
Kazakhstan among youth (17,19,21)


General information about the competition
       From March 23 to 31, 2022 in Nur-Sultan city was held 
Togyzqumalaq Championship of the Republic of Kazakhstan among youth 
(17,19,21), organized by the Ministry of Culture and Sports of the Republic of 
Kazakhstan, the Committee of Sports and Physical Culture, Sports 
Association  Togyzqumala  of the Republic of Kazakhstan and the 
Department of Physical Education and Sports of Nur-Sultan city. The 
competition was attended by 243 athletes from 17 regions, including the cities 
of Nur-Sultan, Almaty, Shymkent.

Chief referee of the competition: M.Shotayev. / Nur-Sultan city. 
General Secretary of the competition: Zh.Issakhanov. /
East.Kaz.reg.

General information about the competition
   Team Togyzqumalaq Championship of the Republic of Kazakhstan among 
men was held from April 13-21 in Uralsk city.
The competition was attended by 80 athletes from 9 regions, including the cities 
of Nur-Sultan, Almaty, Shymkent. Among them: Honored Master of Sports-2, 
International Master of Sports-18, Master of Sports   27.




region.

of the

Selected games of the Togyzqumalaq 
Championship of the Republic of 
Kazakhstan among juniors (9,11,13,15)


General information about the competition
Togyzqumalaq Championship of the Republic of Kazakhstan among juniors 
(9,11,13,15) was held in Almaty city from June 1-10. The competition was
attended by almost 500 athletes from 17 regions, including the cities of Nur- Sultan, 
Almaty, Shymkent. Among them: Candidate Master of Sports-90, I category-184, II 
category  48, III category  9, IV category   42 players.   

Chief	referee	of	the	competition:	A.Kydyrbayev.	/	Almaty	city. 
General Secretary of the competition: M.Nogaibayev. / Almaty city.

Selected games of VII 
People's Togyzqumalaq 
games


General information about the competition
       From June 15 to 20, 2022 in Kostanay city was held     
Togyzqumalaq games, organized by the Ministry of Culture and Sports of the 
Republic of Kazakhstan, the Committee of Sports and Physical Culture, Sports 
Association  Togyzqumala  of the Republic of Kazakhstan and the 
Department of Physical Education and Sports of Kostanay region. The 
competition was attended by 96 athletes from 13 regions, including the cities 
of Nur-Sultan, Almaty, Shymkent. Among them: Honored Master of Sports   
2, International Master of Sports - 18, Master of Sports - 27, Candidate Master 
of Sports - 35, and 14 athletes of I category.
The competition was held in individual and team scoring.


Chief referee of the competition: D.Abdikarimov. / Nur-Sultan city. 
General Secretary of the competition: Zh.Issakhanov. / East.Kaz.reg.

competition:

General information about the competition

   Team Togyzqumalaq Championship of the Republic of Kazakhstan among 
women was held from July 15-23 in Aktobe city.
The competition was attended by 50 athletes from 6 regions. Among them: 
Honored Master of Sports-1, International Master of Sports-18, Master of Sports 
  27.

Chief referee of the competition: N.Kabiyev. / Aktobe region. 
General Secretary of the competition: M.Rakhmetov. /
Kyzylorda region.

      Pavlodar region

region

   	Aktobe region
      Kyzylorda region

     Selected games of 
Kazakhstan Togyzqumalaq Cup


General information about the competition
       From October 3 to 8, 2022 in Karaganda city was held Kazakhstan 
Togyzqumalaq Cup, organized by the Ministry of Culture and Sports of the 
Republic of Kazakhstan, the Committee of Sports and Physical Culture, 
Sports Association  Togyzqumala  of the Republic of Kazakhstan and the 
Department of Physical Education and Sports of Karaganda region. The 
competition was attended by 136 athletes from 17 regions, including the 
cities of Nur-Sultan, Almaty, Shymkent. Among them: Honored Master of 
Sports   2, International Master of Sports - 9, Master of Sports - 14, 
Candidate Master of Sports - 81, and 30 athletes of I category.
The competition was held in individual and team scoring. As a result of the competition, 
Salman Yersultan on 2 board (Turkistan), Turakbay Zhumageldi on 2 board (Mangystau), 
and Ayana Issakhan on 6 board (East.Kaz.reg.) got 1 place and fulfilled the standard of 
 master of sports. 


Chief referee of the competition: Zh.Issakhanov. / East.Kaz.reg. 
General Secretary of the competition: S.Karatay / Karaganda region

  Selected games of the 
VI World Togyzqumalaq
Championship


General information about the competition
From November 20-28, 2022, the VI World Togyzqumalaq Championship was 
held in Aktobe city. It was attended by almost 70 participants from 20 countries of 
the world. The competition was held in three types: Classical, Rapid and Blitz.
Results of competition:
Among men (Classical):
I place - Galymzhan Temirbayev (Kazakhstan)
II place   Beksultan Bostandykov (Kazakhstan)
III place- Anarbek Dzhamakeyev (Kyrgyzstan) 
III place   Oscar Fajardo (Colombia)

Among women (Classical):
I place   Assel Daliyeva (Kazakhstan)
II place - Adina Asseyeva(Kyrgyzstan)
III place   Anssagan Kozhanassip (Kazakhstan) 
III place - Aiturgan Maksatbekkyzy (Kyrgyzstan)

Among men (Blitz):
I place   Asset Kaiyrzhanov (Kazakhstan)
II place   Anarber Dzhamakeyev 
(Kyrgyzstan)
III place   Medet Khussainov (Kazakhstan) 
III place   Marlis Dulatbekov (Kyrgyzstan)

Among women (Blitz):
I place - Gulzhanat Aldabergenova (Kazakhstan)
II place   Aizada Baktybekova (Kyrgyzstan)
III place   Moldir Serikkyzy (Kazakhstan) 
III place   Altynai Shambetova (Kyrgyzstan)

Among men (Rapid):
I place   Asset Kaiyrzhanov (Kazakhstan)
II place - Assylkhan Kozhanassip 
(Kazakhstan)
III place   Nurbek Kabiyev (Kazakhstan)
III place   Yermukhamed Alaidar (Kazakhstan)

Among women (Rapid):
I place - Zhamilya Baildyasheva 
(Kazakhstan)
II place - Assel Daliyeva (Kazakhstan)
III place   Gulnara Bazaraliyeva (Kazakhstan) 
III place - Saltanat Saparbekova (Kazakhstan)

Team scoring:
1.	Kazakhstan - 6 gold, 3 silver, 7 bronze;
2.	Kyrgyzstan - 3 silver, 4 
bronze;
3.	Colombia - 1 bronze.
